	val *= d_cgto_normalization_factors[a->basis_index+2] * d_cgto_normalization_factors[b->basis_index+2] * d_auxiliary_cgto_normalization_factors[c->basis_index+5];
	atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(a->basis_index+2) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+5], val * d_C_diff_vector[(b->basis_index+2)]);
	if(is_prim_id_neq) atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(b->basis_index+2) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+5], val * d_C_diff_vector[(a->basis_index+2)]);

// [pz pz | fxyz]
if ( !((g_upper_bound_factors[abc.x] * g_auxiliary_upper_bound_factors[primitive_index_c] * fabs(d_C_diff_vector[(b->basis_index+2)]) < schwarz_screening_threshold) && (!is_prim_id_neq || g_upper_bound_factors[abc.x] * g_auxiliary_upper_bound_factors[primitive_index_c] * fabs(d_C_diff_vector[(a->basis_index+2)]) < schwarz_screening_threshold))) {
